Let me tell you a little about what I know about support.  You can only support those who have a relationship with you. Any relationship is co-creation (this is a good analogy), which is very demanding on the skills of both people, otherwise, this co-creation can be painful. If people decide to continue a joint relationship (this also applies to friendship), then both people learn a lot to ensure that this joint creativity is of high quality and that this joint creativity brings pleasure to both. Many people do not want to have the difficulties that relationships (including friendship) bring them. Such people make decisions that they do not want to co-create with this person (do not want a certain level of relationship or do not want this level of friendship), so they move away from the other person. And they sacrifice the level of relationships because some of them don't want to figure out how to overcome these difficulties. And along with this, these people refuse certain levels of support from these people. People often look for such people in a relationship with whom they will need to learn minimal things. That is, they are looking for more comfortable people for themselves. Perhaps they are doing the right thing.  Something that I recently learned and that is not written about in books about relationships. When people have a certain level of relationship with each other, then they become, as it were, one whole. And this means, when, according to biorhythms, one of the two is released from psycho toxin (negative feelings and stuff), then this happens through both people. When such a process occurs, then experiences occur in both people. Mutual support (even over a distance, even if it is mental support for each other) is able to remove negative thoughts from both. If a person does not receive something important in a relationship, then both are experiencing a deficit of what is important - each has something of his own.  It is known in nature that binary stars pull each other up to their level (they have the same luminosity, while the luminosity of a small star rises to the luminosity of a large star, while the luminosity of a large star remains at the same level). I assume the same thing happens in relationships. Some kind of restructuring takes place inside a person and both people are pulled up to the upper level of each other. I assume that this process is also uncomfortable and can be painful too.  The very mechanism of support is to take a part of the state of another person upon yourself. Thus, two people divide the state of one of them in half, and each through himself is freed from this.  This is what I know.
Lindsey, thank you for sharing your feelings about this in an interview with Rolling Stone. I congratulate you on overcoming what you chose to overcome.  I have mixed feelings about this video. On the one hand, it is beautiful. On the other hand, you talked about how difficult and painful this creation was for you. The video shows that you do not get pleasure and enjoyment from the process of realizing this creation. This is also part of your creation. And I cannot join those people who see only the outer side of your creation and who do not ask questions about whether you enjoyed it.  Your experience resonates with the experience I had before. I cannot say that this is a positive experience. I used to think that I have a lot of friends. I took care of them as best I could, made creative gifts and drawings. Individually. I wanted these people to spend more time with me, to share something with me just like that. And it took me several years for me to realize that I am not the person with whom they want to spend time. I did a lot of creative work for my friends. Basically, I took the initiative towards them. And they turned to me when they needed something from me. At other times they spent time with their friends, among whom I was not. It seemed to me that what I was doing for them was important to them and that it could make our friendship stronger. I decided to check some things. I decided that I would give my friends the opportunity to take the initiative in the new year and they would wish me a Happy New Year first. On my page, I warned that I would congratulate people later. I congratulated some friends first. I planned this experiment for a year and I knew the result in advance. After the new year, I knew for sure that I have no value for these people. I knew it would happen, but it still hurt. Probably, it was very unpleasant for me that I put my soul and my attitude towards them into the creations for them, and this was not valuable for them.  If I look back at this experience from today's perspective, then I can describe this experience as follows. I called a lot of people my friends, even though these friends treated me like fans treat the artist. An artist makes content for fans, and that content has temporary value for fans. These fans have friends of their own who are of higher value than what the artist does for his fans. A lot of fans don't care what's inside me. If I need support, the fans are the last people to support me. What my fans thought was content from me were my gifts to them. It is clear that such a big difference between what I do and how they perceive it - it had a negative impact on me. And all the same, I needed somewhere 2-3 years to figure out what's what. When my fans decided that there were more important things in their lives than being in my company, they didn't care that it hurt me. They just walked away. And it taught me that the process of creating my art should bring me pleasure. I like to support and I support some friends. Sometimes, it is painful creativity (there are different features that I was able to learn about recently), but this painful process does not go beyond when it has a bad effect on health.  I appreciate you and I do not want you to experience the unpleasant sensations that I went through. I also want to support you on your path, even if you decide to experience such an experience, which may be unpleasant or painful for you.  I am sorry that during this period I did not support you. I think that if I supported you (how it will turn out), then it would be easier for you to go through this experience.

Still even with playback mastering this choreography within 3 months and 24 Lessons from 0 to 100% is very impressive. But it is this speedrun that made the pain.  Yes, the first trainings are painful, but it takes it time and a normal performer uses 3-4 month just to learn hanging full body weight because they need to grow stronger neck muscels and strengthen the body for this. It is important to respect the learning process of the body. Later, if the hair is done properly and the learning time is long enough there is no pain anymore (quoting an artist from circus solei).

I can't stand dance music or dub step. But, two days ago I stumbled upon this video. Since then I have watched the majority of Lindsey's videos, bought Artemis and a bunch of her other work, I've sobbed (Lunar Lullaby), and I checked her tour dates. I am planning on going to see her this summer if I can afford it.   The Arena, Underground, Til the Light Goes Out, Darkside, and Guardian. Those are my personal favorites so far. After a friend's suicide and the Camp fire, I slipped into a deep, dark hole that I have only very recently started clawing my way out of.   Now, after avoiding Lindsey's music for years because of its genre, I am now finding myself relating to it almost more than any other music I've ever heard. Her music has an all too familiar fight in it that I really needed to hear right now. It makes me want to fight too, the way I used to- even more than I used to.   Thank you Lindsey. Thank you.

It is the song that has brought me through my teenage years- through foster care.
